if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '9a761fa824d3b76ba5c26be6ac33be7b1149f734') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '9a761fa824d3b76ba5c26be6ac33be7b1149f734') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '89393d181c55d9409536892fddfad8681f0f8cef') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '9a761fa824d3b76ba5c26be6ac33be7b1149f734') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php') != '5a868da5c4cbe511d355192072986e6b67533818') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php') !== '5a868da5c4cbe511d355192072986e6b67533818') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php') !== '2822d76efadad086ffd0128d44c8acbb846afbc9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/gs1/barcode.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
